# Banglapedia Articles Missing from English Wikipedia

This report lists articles present on the English Banglapedia which do not have a corresponding page on English Wikipedia. This list is extremely useful for identifying gaps in Wikipedia's coverage of Bangladesh-related topics.

## Overview Statistics

| Metric | Value |
| :--- | :--- |
| **Total Banglapedia Articles** | 6,907 |
| **Found on English Wikipedia** | 3,390 |
| **Missing from English Wikipedia** | 3,517 |
| **Coverage Gap (%)** | 50.92% |
